 ' bukamp aane ke baad aae taaja jhatkon, sadakon ke avaruddh hone, bijli gul hone or aspataalon main baari bheed ke kaaran jiviton kaa pataa lagane ke kaam main baadha aa rahi he

 nepal ne is bheeshan aapadaa ke chalate desh main apatsthiti kii ghoshnaa kar di he
 This is the most severe earthquake in the history of the country in the last 80 years
 bharat ne bachaav or punarvaas ke ek bade prayaas ke tahat 13 sainya vimaan tainaat kiye hai, jo asthai aspataal suvidha, dawaaen, kambal or 50 ton pani evam anya saamagree lekar gaye hai
 People from other countries stranded here are waiting impatiently after the earthquake, and the result is that there is chaos at the only international airport

 inamen bhartiya nagarikon kii taadaad sabase adhik he
